Harry admitted, “I didn’t know that could happen.”

Hermione responded,  
- “Nor did I.”  
- “But I suppose if you’re really depressed…”

## Mrs. Weasley and Lunch Call

The door opened, and **Mrs. Weasley** whispered to Ginny,  
- “Ginny, come downstairs and help me with the lunch.”

Ginny protested, “I’m talking to this lot!”

Mrs. Weasley insisted, “Now!” and withdrew.

Ginny complained,  
- “She only wants me there so she doesn’t have to be alone with Phlegm!”  
- She imitated Fleur dramatically and pranced across the room.

Ginny called to the others, “You lot had better come down quickly too.”

## Breakfast and the Telescope

Harry took advantage of the silence to eat more breakfast. Hermione examined **Fred and George's** boxes curiously, occasionally glancing sideways at Harry.

Ron was helping himself to Harry’s toast, still gazing dreamily at the door.

Hermione asked, “What’s this?” holding up a small telescope.

Ron guessed,  
- “Dunno, but if Fred and George left it, it’s probably not ready for the joke shop yet, so be careful.”

Harry remarked, “Your mum said the shop’s going well. Said Fred and George have got a real flair for business.”

Ron bragged,  
- “That’s an understatement.”  
- “They’re raking in the **Galleons**!”  
- “I can’t wait to see the place; we haven’t been to **Diagon Alley** yet.”  
- “Mum says Dad’s got to be there for extra security and he’s been really busy at work.”  
- “But it sounds excellent.”

Harry asked, “And what about Percy? Is he talking to your mum and dad again?”

Ron answered, “Nope.”

Harry noted,  
- “But he knows your dad was right all along now about **Voldemort** being back…”

Hermione quoted **Dumbledore**,  
- “People find it far easier to forgive others for being wrong than being right.”  
- “I heard him telling your mum, Ron.”

Ron commented,  
- “Sounds like the sort of mental thing Dumbledore would say.”

Harry shared,  
- “He’s going to be giving me private lessons this year.”

Ron choked on his toast, and Hermione gasped.

Ron said impressed,  
- “You kept that quiet!”  
- “Blimey… private lessons with Dumbledore!”  
- “I wonder why he’s…?”

Harry saw the exchanged looks between Ron and Hermione.

He laid down his knife and fork, heart beating fast.

He said,  
- “I don’t know exactly why he’s going to be giving me lessons, but I think it must be because of the **prophecy**.”

Ron and Hermione froze.

Harry continued,  
- “You know, the one they were trying to steal at the Ministry.”

Hermione said quickly,  
- “Nobody knows what it said, though. It got smashed.”

Ron started, “Although the Prophet says…” but Hermione shushed him.

Harry insisted,  
- “The Prophet’s got it right.”  
- “That glass ball that smashed wasn’t the only record of the prophecy.”  
- “I heard the whole thing in Dumbledore’s office, he was the one the prophecy was made to, so he could tell me.”  
- “From what it said, it looks like I’m the one who’s got to finish off Voldemort…”  
- “At least, it said neither of us could live while the other survives.”

The three stared in silence.

Suddenly, there was a loud bang and Hermione vanished behind a puff of black smoke.

## Hermione’s Incident with the Telescope

Hermione emerged, coughing and clutching the telescope, sporting a brilliantly **purple black eye**.

She gasped,  
- “I squeezed it and it… it punched me!”

They saw a tiny fist on a long spring protruding from the telescope.

Ron laughed and reassured,  
- “Don’t worry, Mum’ll fix that, she’s good at healing minor injuries…”

Hermione hurried on,  
- “Oh well, never mind that now! Harry, oh, Harry…”

She sat on the edge of his bed again.

## Thoughts on the Prophecy and Fear

Hermione explained,  
- “We wondered, after we got back from the Ministry…”  
- “We didn’t want to say anything to you, but from what **Lucius Malfoy** said about the prophecy…”  
- “Well, we thought it might be something like this.”  
- She asked quietly, “Are you scared?”

Harry answered,  
- “Not as much as I was.”  
- “When I first heard it, I was… but now, it seems as though I always knew I’d have to face him in the end…”

Ron said eagerly,  
- “When we heard Dumbledore was collecting you in person, we thought he might be telling or showing you something about the prophecy.”  
- “And we were kind of right, weren’t we?”  
- “He wouldn’t be giving you lessons if he thought you were a goner, wouldn’t waste his time.”  
- “He must think you’ve got a chance!”

Hermione speculated,  
- “I wonder what he’ll teach you, Harry?”  
- “Really advanced defensive magic, powerful countercurses, anti-jinxes…”

Harry was distracted but felt a warmth inside.

He appreciated that Ron and Hermione stayed with him, speaking words of comfort and not shirking away.

Hermione added,  
- “…and evasive enchantments generally.”  
- “Well, at least you know one lesson you’ll be having this year, that’s one more than Ron and me.”  
- “I wonder when our **O.W.L.** results will come?”

Ron replied, “Can’t be long now, it’s been a month.”

Harry recalled,  
- “I think Dumbledore said our O.W.L. results would be arriving today!”

Hermione shrieked,  
- “Today? But why didn’t you… oh my God… you should have said…”

She leapt to her feet.

## Hermione’s Bruise: A Joke Gone Wrong

When Harry arrived downstairs ten minutes later, fully dressed and carrying his empty breakfast tray, he found Hermione sitting at the kitchen table in great agitation.

**Mrs. Weasley** was trying to lessen her resemblance to half a panda.

Mrs. Weasley said anxiously,  
- “It just won’t budge.”  
- “This has always worked before, I just can’t understand it.”

Hermione exclaimed,  
- “It’ll be Fred and George’s idea of a funny joke.”  
- “Making sure it can’t come off.”

Hermione fretted,  
- “But it’s got to come off!”  
- “I can’t go around looking like this forever!”

Mrs. Weasley soothed,  
- “You won’t, dear, we’ll find an antidote, don’t worry.”

Fleur smiled serenely,  
- “Bill told me Fred and George are very amusing!”

Hermione snapped, “Yes, I can hardly breathe for laughing.”

She jumped up and started pacing the kitchen, twisting her fingers.

Hermione anxiously asked Mrs. Weasley,  
- “You’re quite, quite sure no owls have arrived this morning?”

Mrs. Weasley replied patiently,  
- “Yes, dear, I’d have noticed.”  
- “But it’s barely nine, there’s still plenty of time…”

## Concerns about O.W.L. Results

Hermione muttered feverishly,  
- “I know I messed up **Ancient Runes**.”  
- “I definitely made at least one serious mistranslation.”  
- “The **Defense Against the Dark Arts** practical was no good at all.”  
- “I thought **Transfiguration** went all right at the time, but looking back…”

Ron barked,  
- “Hermione, will you shut up, you’re not the only one who’s nervous!”  
- “And when you’ve got your eleven 'Outstanding O.W.L.s…'”

Hermione flapped her hands hysterically,  
- “Don’t, don’t, don’t!”  
- “I know I’ve failed everything!”

Harry asked,  
- “What happens if we fail?”

Hermione answered,  
- “We discuss our options with our **Head of House**.”  
- “I asked **Professor McGonagall** at the end of last term.”

Harry felt nervous and wished he had eaten less for breakfast.

## Fleur’s Comparison with Beauxbatons

Fleur said complacently,  
- “At **Beauxbatons**, we had a different way of doing things.”  
- “I think it was better.”  
- "We sat our examinations after six years of study, not five, and then..."

Her words were drowned in a scream.

## Arrival of O.W.L. Results by Owl Post

Hermione pointed through the kitchen window.

Three black specks were visible in the sky, growing larger rapidly.

Ron exclaimed hoarsely,  
- “They’re definitely owls.”

Harry joined Hermione at the window.

Hermione whispered terrified,  
- “There are three of them.”  
- “One for each of us.”  
- “Oh no… oh no… oh no…”

She gripped both Harry and Ron tightly around the elbows.

## Harry’s O.W.L. Results

The **owls** were flying directly at the **Burrow**, three handsome tawnies, each carrying a large square envelope. Mrs. Weasley opened the kitchen window, and all three owls soared through it, landing on the table in a neat line, each lifting their right leg.

Harry moved forward to untie the letter addressed to him. To his left, Ron was trying to detach his results; to his right, Hermione’s hands were shaking, making her owl tremble. Nobody in the kitchen spoke.

Harry slit open the envelope and unfolded the parchment inside.

### Ordinary Wizarding Level Results

**Pass Grades:**

- **Outstanding (O)**
- **Exceeds Expectations (E)**
- **Acceptable (A)**

**Fail Grades:**

- **Poor (P)**
- **Dreadful (D)**
- **Troll (T)**

### Harry James Potter’s O.W.L. Grades:

- **Astronomy**: A
- **Care of Magical Creatures**: E
- **Charms**: E
- **Defense Against the Dark Arts**: O
- **Divination**: P
- **Herbology**: E
- **History of Magic**: D
- **Potions**: E
- **Transfiguration**: E

Harry read the parchment multiple times, feeling his breathing ease. He was relieved—he had expected to fail **Divination** and **History of Magic**, having collapsed during the History exam, but he had passed everything else. He was especially proud of his **Outstanding** at **Defense Against the Dark Arts**.

Ron looked delighted and said, “Only failed Divination and History of Magic, and who cares about them?” He teased Harry about swapping results, noting he had no **Outstandings**.

Mrs. Weasley proudly ruffled Ron’s hair, saying, “Seven O.W.L.s, that’s more than Fred and George got together!”

### Hermione’s Results

Hermione hadn’t turned around initially. When asked, she said, “I—not bad.” Ron revealed she had **ten ‘Outstandings’** and one **‘Exceeds Expectations’** at **Defense Against the Dark Arts**.

Ron joked about Hermione being disappointed, but Harry laughed.

Ron grinned, “Well, we’re N.E.W.T. students now!”

Mrs. Weasley chimed in, “Mum, are there any more sausages?”

Harry glanced back down at his results, feeling content but with a slight regret. His ambition to become an **Auror** ended here; he had not secured the needed **Potions** grade. The small black **E** was a sinking reality.

He reflected on how a **Death Eater in disguise** had told him he'd make a good Auror, and the prophecy “Neither can live while the other survives” made the choice seem like the right destiny.

---

## 6. DRACO’S DETOUR 

Harry spent his holidays mostly in the **Burrow’s garden**, playing two-a-side **Quidditch** (himself and Hermione vs. Ron and Ginny). Hermione was dreadful at Quidditch, Ginny good, making the teams balanced. Evenings were filled with **Mrs. Weasley’s triple helpings** of food.

However, the holiday was marred by grim news—Disappearances, odd accidents, and deaths were almost daily in the **Daily Prophet**. Bill and Mr. Weasley often brought news earlier than the paper.

At Harry’s sixteenth birthday, the mood was dark. **Remus Lupin**, looking gaunt and grim with gray streaks in his hair, brought tidings of:

- New **Dementor attacks**
- The discovery of **Igor Karkaroff’s body** with a **Dark Mark** over it

Mrs. Weasley tried to change the subject, but discussions turned to other missing figures.

### News from Diagon Alley

- **Florean Fortescue**, a kind man who ran the **ice-cream place**, had been forcibly taken.
- **Ollivander**, the renowned **wandmaker**, had disappeared; his shop was empty with no sign of struggle.
- This raised concerns about what people would do for wands.

Lupin explained Ollivander was the best, and if he had been captured, it was bad news for the others.

### Hogwarts Letters and Booklists

The day after the gloomy birthday tea, letters and booklists arrived from **Hogwarts**.

Harry’s letter brought a surprise—he had been made **Quidditch Captain**.

Hermione was excited, saying, “That gives you equal status with prefects! You can use our special bathroom now!”

Ron was thrilled, hoping Harry would let him back on the team. Mrs. Weasley planned a trip to **Diagon Alley** for supplies but insisted Mr. Weasley come along, showing her concern for security.

Ron tried to joke about Voldemort hiding in shops, but Mrs. Weasley warned against treating security lightly.

### Preparations for Diagon Alley

Bill gave Harry a bag of **gold** from his vault, explaining that getting gold had become difficult due to tightened goblin security.

The day of the trip dawned overcast. A special **Ministry of Magic car** waited for them. Mr. and Mrs. Weasley sat in front with the Ministry driver, and Harry, Ron, Hermione, and Ginny sat in the back.

Mr. Weasley said Harry had **top-grade security status**, and additional security would join them at the **Leaky Cauldron**.

Harry felt uneasy about being surrounded by **Aurors** while shopping but brought his **Invisibility Cloak**, thinking if Dumbledore used it, it should be sufficient.

### Arrival at the Leaky Cauldron

At the **Leaky Cauldron**, no Aurors were waiting; instead, they saw **Rubeus Hagrid**, the **Hogwarts gamekeeper**, wearing a beaverskin coat, beaming at Harry.

Hagrid greeted Harry with a strong hug, telling him about **Buckbeak (Witherwings)**, glad to be back outside.

Despite Ministry plans to send Aurors, Dumbledore insisted that Hagrid come instead.

The Leaky Cauldron was empty except for **Tom the landlord**, who looked hopeful as they entered. Hagrid told Tom they were "just passing through" for Hogwarts business.

They walked through the bar and out into the chilly courtyard where Hagrid revealed a secret entrance to a winding cobbled street.

---

# End of text provided.

## Diagon Alley Changes

**Diagon Alley** had changed significantly. The colorful, glittering **window displays** of **spellbooks**, **potion ingredients**, and **cauldrons** were hidden behind large **Ministry of Magic** posters. Most posters displayed **security advice** taken from Ministry pamphlets, but others showed moving black-and-white photographs of **Death Eaters** known to be at large.

- **Bellatrix Lestrange** sneered from the front of the nearest apothecary.
- Several windows, including **Florean Fortescue’s Ice Cream Parlor**, were boarded up.
- Shabby stalls appeared, such as one outside **Flourish and Blotts** with a cardboard sign advertising:

  **AMULETS**

  *Effective Against Werewolves, Dementors, and Inferi!*

A seedy wizard rattled silver amulets on chains, calling out to passersby.

---

## The Weasley Family and Diagon Alley

Mrs. Weasley was nervous but insisted on completing school shopping quickly:

- Hermione needed new dress robes.
- Ron’s school robes showed too much ankle.
- Harry needed new robes due to growth.

Mr. Weasley suggested splitting up:

- Harry, Ron, Hermione, and Hagrid would go to **Madam Malkin’s**.
- The rest would shop at **Flourish and Blotts** for schoolbooks.

Mrs. Weasley reluctantly agreed as Hagrid offered to stand guard outside Madam Malkin’s.

---

## Encounter at Madam Malkin’s

Inside Madam Malkin’s shop, Harry, Ron, and Hermione heard familiar voices. 

- **Draco Malfoy**, in dark green robes, insulted Hermione, calling her a **Mudblood**.
- **Madam Malkin** scolded Draco and forbade drawing wands in her shop.
- Harry and Ron raised their wands but were ordered to lower them by **Narcissa Malfoy**.

### Confrontation Details

- Narcissa threatened Harry, warning him not to attack Draco again.
- Harry taunted her, disregarding her warning.
- Malfoy threw his robes on the floor and left with Narcissa, bumping Ron deliberately.
- Madam Malkin resumed fitting robes but seemed eager to be done with them.

---

## After Madam Malkin’s

Hagrid reassured the trio that the Malfoys would not cause trouble in public.

- Mr. and Mrs. Weasley, along with Ginny, returned with heavy packages.
- The group visited the **Apothecary** and **Eeylops Owl Emporium**.
- Harry and Ron bought large boxes of owl nuts for **Hedwig** and **Pigwidgeon**.

Mrs. Weasley, anxious to finish shopping, led the group toward **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**, the joke shop run by **Fred and George**.

---

## Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes

The shop’s windows stood out brightly amidst the dull surroundings:

- One window displayed goods that revolved, popped, flashed, bounced, and shrieked.
- The other showed a giant purple poster:

  **WHY ARE YOU WORRYING ABOUT YOU-KNOW-WHO?  
  YOU SHOULD BE WORRYING ABOUT U-NO-POO—  
  THE CONSTIPATION SENSATION THAT’S GRIPPING THE NATION!**

This made Harry and Ron laugh, while Mrs. Weasley was visibly shocked.

### Inside the Shop

- The shop was packed with customers; Harry struggled to get near shelves.
- Boxes piled to the ceiling included **Skiving Snackboxes**, perfected by the twins.
- **Nosebleed Nougat** was the most popular item, with only one battered box left.
- There were bins of **trick wands** ranging from harmless rubber chickens to dangerous.
- Boxes of quills came in **Self-Inking**, **Spell-Checking**, and **Smart-Answer** varieties.
- A crowd watched a miniature wooden man climb "Reusable hangman" gallows with the warning:  
  *spell it or he’ll swing!*

---

## Hermione and the Daydream Charms

Hermione read the back of a **Daydream Charms** box showing a pirate ship scene:

> “One simple incantation and you will enter a top-quality, highly realistic, thirty-minute daydream, easy to fit into the average school lesson and virtually undetectable (side effects include vacant expression and minor drooling). Not for sale to under-sixteens.”

She remarked on the extraordinary magic involved.

---

## Meeting Fred Weasley

Fred appeared wearing magenta robes and greeted Harry and Hermione warmly:

- Fred noticed Hermione’s black eye.
- Handed her a tub of thick yellow paste as a **bruise remover**.
- Explained most products were tested on themselves.
- Hermione hesitated, asking if it was safe.

## Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes Tour

“’Course it is,” said **Fred** bracingly. “Come on, **Harry**, I’ll give you a tour.”

**Harry** left **Hermione** dabbing her black eye with paste and followed **Fred** toward the back of the shop, where he saw a stand of **card and rope tricks**.

- “**Muggle magic tricks**!” said **Fred** happily, pointing them out. “For freaks like **Dad**, you know, who love **Muggle** stuff. It’s not a big earner, but we do fairly steady business, they’re great novelties…”

- “Oh, here’s **George**…”  

**Fred’s** twin shook **Harry’s** hand energetically.

- “Giving him the tour? Come through the back, **Harry**, that’s where we’re making the real money… pocket anything, you, and you’ll pay in more than **Galleons**!” he added warningly to a small boy who hastily whipped his hand out of the tub labeled: **Edible Dark Marks—They’ll Make Anyone Sick!**

**George** pushed back a curtain beside the Muggle tricks and **Harry** saw a darker, less crowded room. The packaging on the products lining these shelves was more subdued.

- “We’ve just developed this more serious line,” said **Fred**. “Funny how it happened…”

### Shield Charm Products

- “You wouldn’t believe how many people, even people who work at the **Ministry**, can’t do a decent **Shield Charm**,” said **George**. “’Course, they didn’t have you teaching them, **Harry**.”

- “That’s right… Well, we thought **Shield Hats** were a bit of a laugh, you know, challenge your mate to jinx you while wearing it and watch his face when the jinx just bounces off. But the **Ministry** bought five hundred for all its support staff! And we’re still getting massive orders!”

- “So we’ve expanded into a range of **Shield Cloaks**, **Shield Gloves**…”

- “…I mean, they wouldn’t help much against the **Unforgivable Curses**, but for minor to moderate hexes or jinxes…”

### Defense Against the Dark Arts Products

- “And then we thought we’d get into the whole area of **Defense Against the Dark Arts**, because it’s such a money spinner,” continued **George** enthusiastically.

- “This is cool. Look, **Instant Darkness Powder**, we’re importing it from **Peru**. Handy if you want to make a quick escape.”

- “And our **Decoy Detonators** are just walking off the shelves, look,” said **Fred**, pointing at a number of weird-looking black horn-type objects.

- “You just drop one surreptitiously and it’ll run off and make a nice loud noise out of sight, giving you a diversion if you need one.”

- “Handy,” said **Harry**, impressed.

- “Here,” said **George**, catching a couple and throwing them to **Harry**.

### Customer Interaction

A young witch with short blonde hair poked her head around the curtain; she was wearing **magenta staff robes**.

- “There’s a customer out here looking for a **joke cauldron**, Mr. Weasley and Mr. Weasley,” she said.

**Fred** and **George** took being called “Mr. Weasley” in their stride.

- “Right you are, **Verity**, I’m coming,” said **George** promptly. “**Harry**, you help yourself to anything you want, all right? No charge.”

- “I can’t do that!” said **Harry**, pulling out his money bag to pay for the **Decoy Detonators**.

- “You don’t pay here,” said **Fred** firmly, waving away **Harry’s gold**.

- “You gave

## Borgin and Burkes Incident

Next moment, the bell over the door tinkled loudly as **Malfoy** stalked out of the shop looking very pleased with himself. He passed so close to **Harry**, **Ron**, and **Hermione** that they felt the cloak flutter around their knees again. Inside the shop, **Borgin** remained frozen; his unctuous smile had vanished; he looked worried.

- Ron whispered, “What was that about?” while reeling in the **Extendable Ears**.
- Harry thought hard: “He wants something mended… and he wants to reserve something in there… Could you see what he pointed at when he said ‘that one’?”
- Ron replied, “No, he was behind that cabinet…”

Hermione told them, “You two stay here,” then ducked out from under the cloak, checked her hair in the reflection, and marched into the shop, setting the bell tinkling again.

Hermione greeted Borgin cheerily, “Hello, horrible morning, isn’t it?” Borgin did not answer but cast her a suspicious look.

Hermione asked about items on display:

- **Necklace**: “If you’ve got one and a half thousand Galleons,” said Borgin coldly.
- **Skull**: “Sixteen Galleons.”

Hermione probed if the skull was kept for anyone but Borgin squinted suspiciously. Hermione then tried a bluff:

> “The thing is, that—er—boy who was in here just now, **Draco Malfoy**, well, he’s a friend of mine, and I want to get him a birthday present, but if he’s already reserved anything, I obviously don’t want to get him the same thing…”

Borgin cut her off sharply: “Out. Get out!”

Hermione hurried to the door with Borgin at her heels. The bell tinkled again, Borgin slammed the door, and put up the closed sign.

Ron remarked, “Worth a try, but you were a bit obvious…”

Hermione snapped back, “Well, next time you can show me how it’s done, Master of Mystery!”

They bickered on the way back to **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**, dodging the suspicious glances of **Mrs. Weasley** and **Hagrid**. Once inside, Harry removed the **Invisibility Cloak**, hid it in his bag, and joined the others when they insisted to Mrs. Weasley that they had been in the back room all along.

---

## 7. THE SLUG CLUB

Harry spent much of the last week of the holidays pondering **Malfoy’s behavior** in Knockturn Alley. What disturbed him most was the **satisfied look** on Malfoy’s face after leaving the shop. Nothing that made Malfoy happy could be good news.

- Hermione was less curious and got bored discussing it.
- Hermione: “Haven’t we agreed there could be many explanations?”
- Ron vaguely suggested Malfoy might need to fix his **Hand of Glory**.
- Harry pressed the point about Malfoy saying, “Don’t forget to keep that one safe,” implying Borgin had two broken objects.

Harry speculated, “Malfoy’s father’s in **Azkaban**. Don’t you think Malfoy’d like revenge?”

Ron looked skeptical: “Malfoy, revenge? What can he do about it?”

Harry persisted, “He’s a **Death Eater** and...”

Suddenly Harry noticed Hermione’s face and Ron’s nervous reaction.

- Hermione anxiously asked if Harry’s scar was hurting.
- Harry claimed, “He’s replaced his father as a Death Eater!”

Ron laughed, “He’s sixteen, Harry! You think **You-Know-Who** would let Malfoy join?”

Hermione was unsure: “What makes you think...?”

Harry explained:

- Madam Malkin tried to touch Malfoy’s left arm.
- Malfoy jerked it away.
- Harry believed Malfoy was **branded with the Dark Mark**.
- Borgin was seriously scared when Malfoy showed him something unseen.

Ron and Hermione exchanged doubtful looks but Harry was convinced.

Annoyed but determined, Harry snatched some filthy **Quidditch robes** to do laundry.

---

## Kitchen Scene and Departure Preparations

In the kitchen, Harry found **Fleur** planning her wedding with **Mrs. Weasley**.

- Fleur discussed bridesmaids’ dresses and hair colors.
- Mrs. Weasley provided updates on **security arrangements** for the journey to Hogwarts.
- Ministry cars and **Aurors** would escort them.
- **Tonks** was not expected to be there.
- Mrs. Weasley stressed the importance of having trunks ready.

Their departure next morning was smooth.

- Ministry cars arrived.
- Trunks were packed.
- **Hermione's cat Crookshanks**, **Hedwig**, **Ron’s owl Pigwidgeon**, and **Ginny’s Pygmy Puff Arnold** were caged.
- **Fleur** kissed Harry goodbye.
- Ron fell awkwardly at Fleur’s feet after Ginny tripped him.

---

## Arrival at King's Cross Station

No cheerful **Hagrid** greeted them. Instead, two grim-faced **Aurors** in Muggle suits escorted them wordlessly into the station.

Mrs. Weasley was flustered but guided them onward.

- The Auror tried to physically usher Harry through the barrier between platforms nine and ten.
- Harry resisted and walked through by himself.
- Hermione and the Weasleys joined him.
- Hermione and Ron had to visit the prefects’ carriage and then patrol the corridors.
- Mrs. Weasley reminded them to board quickly.

---

## Harry’s Conversation with Mr. Weasley

Harry decided to speak privately with **Mr. Weasley** because:

- Mr. Weasley worked at the Ministry.
- He could investigate safely.
- He was less likely to react with anger.

Mrs. Weasley and the Auror watched suspiciously as Harry and Mr. Weasley moved out of earshot.

Harry confessed:

- They followed **Draco Malfoy** using the **Invisibility Cloak**.
- Malfoy had bullied Borgin in **Borgin and Burkes**.
- He wanted something fixed and reserved something else.
- Malfoy was likely branded with the **Dark Mark**.
- Harry feared Malfoy had replaced his father as a **Death Eater**.

Mr. Weasley looked taken aback.

- He doubted that **You-Know-Who** would allow a sixteen-year-old into the Death Eaters.

## Train Journey and Suspicion

“Does anyone really know what **You-Know-Who** would or wouldn’t do?” asked **Harry** angrily. “**Mr. Weasley**, I’m sorry, but isn’t it worth investigating? If **Malfoy** wants something fixing, and he needs to threaten **Borgin** to get it done, it’s probably something **Dark** or dangerous, isn’t it?”

“I doubt it, to be honest, Harry,” said **Mr. Weasley** slowly. “You see, when **Lucius Malfoy** was arrested, we raided his house. We took away everything that might have been dangerous.”

“I think you missed something,” said **Harry** stubbornly.

“Well, maybe,” said **Mr. Weasley**, but Harry could tell that Mr. Weasley was humoring him.

There was a whistle behind them; nearly everyone had boarded the train and the doors were closing.

“You’d better hurry!” said **Mr. Weasley**, as **Mrs. Weasley** cried, “Harry, quickly!”

## Boarding the Train

He hurried forward and **Mr. and Mrs. Weasley** helped him load his trunk onto the train.

“Now, dear, you’re coming to us for **Christmas**, it’s all fixed with **Dumbledore**, so we’ll see you quite soon,” said **Mrs. Weasley** through the window, as Harry slammed the door shut behind him and the train began to move. “You make sure you look after yourself and—”

The train was gathering speed.

“—be good and—”

She was jogging to keep up now.

“—stay safe!”

Harry waved until the train had turned a corner and **Mr. and Mrs. Weasley** were lost to view, then turned to see where the others had got to. He supposed **Ron** and **Hermione** were cloistered in the prefects’ carriage, but **Ginny** was a little way along the corridor, chatting to some friends. He made his way toward her, dragging his trunk.

## Staring Students and Friends

People stared shamelessly as he approached. They even pressed their faces against the windows of their compartments to get a look at him. He had expected an upswing in the amount of gaping and gawping he would have to endure this term after all the “**Chosen One**” rumors in the **Daily Prophet**, but he did not enjoy the sensation of standing in a very bright spotlight. He tapped **Ginny** on the shoulder.

“Fancy trying to find a compartment?”

“I can’t, Harry, I said I’d meet **Dean**,” said **Ginny** brightly. “See you later.”

“Right,” said **Harry**. He felt a strange twinge of annoyance as she walked away, her long red hair dancing behind her; he had become so used to her presence over the summer that he had almost forgotten that Ginny did not hang around with him, Ron, and Hermione while at school.

Then he blinked and looked around: He was surrounded by mesmerized girls.

## Reunion with Neville and Luna

“Hi, Harry!” said a familiar voice from behind him.

“**Neville**!” said Harry in relief, turning to see a round-faced boy struggling toward him.

“Hello, Harry,” said a girl with long hair and large misty eyes, who was just behind Neville.

“**Luna**, hi, how are you?”

“Very well, thank you,” said **Luna**. She was clutching a magazine to her chest; large letters on the front announced that there was a pair of free **Spectrespecs** inside.

“The **Quibbler** still going strong, then?” asked Harry, who felt a certain fondness for the magazine, having given it an exclusive interview the previous year.

“Oh yes, circulation’s well up,” said **Luna** happily.

“Let’s find seats,” said Harry, and the three of them set off along the train through hordes of silently staring students. At last they found an empty compartment, and Harry hurried inside gratefully.

“They’re even staring at us,” said **Neville**, indicating himself and Luna. “Because we’re with you!”

## Discussion About D.A.

“They’re staring at you because you were at the **Ministry** too,” said Harry, as he hoisted his trunk into the luggage rack. “Our little adventure there was all over the **Daily Prophet**, you must’ve seen it.”

“Yes, I thought **Gran** would be angry about all the publicity,” said Neville, “but she was really pleased. Says I’m starting to live up to my dad at long last. She bought me a new wand, look!”

He pulled it out and showed it to Harry.

“**Cherry and unicorn hair**,” he said proudly. “We think it was one of the last **Ollivander** ever sold, he vanished next day… oi, come back here, Trevor!”

And he dived under the seat to retrieve his toad as it made one of its frequent bids for freedom.

“Are we still doing **D.A. meetings** this year, Harry?” asked Luna, who was detaching a pair of psychedelic spectacles from the middle of **The Quibbler**.

“No point now we’ve got rid of **Umbridge**, is there?” said Harry, sitting down

## Slughorn’s Lunch Invitation

Neville nodded, looking scared. At a gesture from **Slughorn**, they sat down opposite each other in the only two empty seats, which were nearest the door. Harry glanced around at their fellow guests. He recognized a **Slytherin** from their year, a tall black boy with high cheekbones and long, slanting eyes; there were also two seventh-year boys Harry did not know and, squashed in the corner beside Slughorn and looking as though she was not entirely sure how she had got there, **Ginny**.

“Now, do you know everyone?” Slughorn asked Harry and Neville. “**Blaise Zabini** is in your year, of course—”

Zabini did not make any sign of recognition or greeting, nor did Harry or Neville: **Gryffindor** and **Slytherin** students loathed each other on principle.

“This is **Cormac McLaggen**, perhaps you’ve come across each other—? No?”

McLaggen, a large, wiry-haired youth, raised a hand, and Harry and Neville nodded back at him.

“—and this is **Marcus Belby**, I don’t know whether—?”

Belby, who was thin and nervous-looking, gave a strained smile.

“—and this charming young lady tells me she knows you!” Slughorn finished.

Ginny grimaced at Harry and Neville from behind Slughorn’s back.

“Well now, this is most pleasant,” said Slughorn cozily. “A chance to get to know you all a little better. Here, take a napkin. I’ve packed my own lunch; the trolley, as I remember it, is heavy on licorice wands, and a poor old man’s digestive system isn’t quite up to such things… Pheasant, Belby?”

Belby started and accepted what looked like half a cold pheasant.

## Slughorn’s Conversations and Interactions

“I was just telling young Marcus here that I had the pleasure of teaching his **Uncle Damocles**,” Slughorn told Harry and Neville, now passing around a basket of rolls. “Outstanding wizard, outstanding, and his **Order of Merlin** most well-deserved. Do you see much of your uncle, Marcus?”

Unfortunately, Belby had just taken a large mouthful of pheasant; in his haste to answer Slughorn he swallowed too fast, turned purple, and began to choke.

“**Anapneo**,” said Slughorn calmly, pointing his wand at Belby, whose airway seemed to clear at once.

“Not… not much of him, no,” gasped Belby, his eyes streaming.

“Well, of course, I daresay he’s busy,” said Slughorn, looking questioningly at Belby. “I doubt he invented the **Wolfsbane Potion** without considerable hard work!”

“I suppose…” said Belby, who seemed afraid to take another bite of pheasant until he was sure that Slughorn had finished with him. “Er… he and my dad don’t get on very well, you see, so I don’t really know much about…”

His voice tailed away as Slughorn gave him a cold smile and turned to McLaggen instead.

“Now, you, Cormac,” said Slughorn, “I happen to know you see a lot of your **Uncle Tiberius**, because he has a rather splendid picture of the two of you hunting **nogtails** in, I think, Norfolk?”

“Oh, yeah, that was fun, that was,” said McLaggen. “We went with **Bertie Higgs** and **Rufus Scrimgeour**; this was before he became Minister, obviously…”

“Ah, you know Bertie and Rufus too?” beamed Slughorn, now offering around a small tray of pies; somehow, Belby was missed out. “Now tell me…”

## The "Slug Club" Guests and Backgrounds

It was as Harry had suspected. Everyone here seemed to have been invited because they were connected to somebody well-known or influential… everyone except Ginny. Zabini, who was interrogated after McLaggen, turned out to have a famously beautiful witch for a mother (from what Harry could make out, she had been married seven times, each of her husbands dying mysteriously and leaving her mounds of gold).

It was Neville’s turn next: This was a very uncomfortable ten minutes, for Neville’s parents, well-known **Aurors**, had been tortured into insanity by **Bellatrix Lestrange** and a couple of Death Eater cronies. At the end of Neville’s interview, Harry had the impression that Slughorn was reserving judgment on Neville, yet to see whether he had any of his parents’ flair.

## Slughorn and Harry Potter

“And now,” said Slughorn, shifting massively in his seat with the air of a compere introducing his star act. “**Harry Potter**! Where to begin? I feel I barely scratched the surface when we met over the summer!” He contemplated Harry for a moment as though he was a particularly large and succulent piece of pheasant, then said, “‘The **Chosen One**,’ they’re calling you now!”

Harry said nothing. Belby, McLaggen, and Zabini were all staring at him.

“Of course,” said Slughorn, watching Harry closely, “there have been rumors for years… I remember when—well—after that terrible night—**Lily**—**James**—and you survived—and the word was that you must have powers beyond the ordinary—”

Zabini gave a tiny little cough that was clearly supposed to indicate amused skepticism. An angry voice burst out from behind Slughorn.

“Yeah, Zabini, because you’re so talented… at posing…”

“Oh dear!” chuckled Slughorn comfortably, looking around at Ginny, who was glaring at Zabini around Slughorn’s great belly. “You want to be careful, Blaise! I saw this young lady perform the most marvelous **Bat-Bogey Hex** as I was passing her carriage! I wouldn’t cross her!”

Zabini merely looked contemptuous.

“Anyway,” said Slughorn, turning back to Harry. “Such rumors this summer. Of course, one doesn’t know what to believe, the **Prophet** has been known to print inaccuracies, make mistakes… but there seems little doubt, given the number of witnesses, that there was quite a disturbance at the **Ministry** and that you were there in the thick of it all!”

Harry, who could not see any way out of this without flatly lying, nodded but still said nothing. Slughorn beamed at him.

“So modest, so modest, no wonder **Dumbledore** is so fond… you were there, then? But the rest of the stories—so sensational, of course, one doesn’t know quite what to believe… this fabled prophecy, for instance—”

“We never heard a prophecy,” said Neville, turning geranium pink as he said it.

“That’s right,” said Ginny staunchly. “Neville and I were both there too, and all this ‘Chosen One’ rubbish is just the **Prophet** making things up as usual.”

“You were both there too, were you?” said Slughorn with great interest, looking from Ginny to Neville, but both of them sat clam-like before his encouraging smile.

“Yes… well… it is true that the **Prophet** often exaggerates, of course…” Slughorn said, sounding a little disappointed. “I remember dear **Gwenog** telling me (**Gwenog Jones**, I mean, of course, Captain of the **Holyhead Harpies**)—”

He meandered off into a long-winded reminiscence, but Harry had the distinct impression that Slughorn had not finished with him, and that he had not been convinced by Neville and Ginny.

## The Slug Club’s Atmosphere and Departure

The afternoon wore on with more anecdotes about illustrious wizards Slughorn had taught, all of whom had been delighted to join what he called the “**Slug Club**” at Hogwarts. Harry could not wait to leave, but couldn’t see how to do so politely.

Finally the train emerged from yet another long misty stretch into a red sunset, and Slughorn looked around, blinking in the twilight.

“Good gracious, it’s getting dark already! I didn’t notice that they’d lit the lamps! You’d better go and change into your robes, all of you. McLaggen, you must drop by and borrow that book on nogtails. Harry, Blaise… any time you’re passing. Same goes for you, miss,” he twinkled at Ginny. “Well, off you go, off you go!”

As he pushed past Harry into the darkening corridor, Zabini shot him a filthy look that Harry returned with interest. He, Ginny, and Neville followed Zabini back along the train.

“I’m glad that’s over,” muttered Neville. “Strange man, isn’t he?”

“Yeah, he is a bit,” said Harry, his eyes on Zabini. “How come you ended up in there, Ginny?”

“He saw me hex **Zacharias Smith**,” said Ginny. “You remember that idiot from **Hufflepuff** who was in the **D.A.**? He kept on and on asking about what happened at the Ministry and in the end he annoyed me so much I hexed him—when Slughorn came in I thought I was going to got detention, but he just thought it was a really good hex and invited me to lunch! Mad, eh?”

“Better reason for inviting someone than because their mother’s famous,” said Harry, scowling at the back of Zabini’s head, “or because their uncle…”

But he broke off. An idea had just occurred to him, a reckless but potentially wonderful idea… In a minute’s time, Zabini was going to reenter the **Slytherin sixth-year compartment** and **Malfoy** would be sitting there, thinking himself unheard by anybody except fellow Slytherins… If Harry could only enter, unseen, behind him, what might he not see or hear?

True, there was little of the journey left—**Hogsmeade Station** had to be less than half an hour away, judging by the wildness of the scenery flashing by the windows—but nobody else seemed prepared to take Harry’s suspicions seriously, so it was down to him to prove them.

## Harry’s Covert Operation

“I’ll see you two later,” said Harry under his breath, pulling out his **Invisibility Cloak** and flinging it over himself.

“But what’re you—?” asked Neville.

“Later!” whispered Harry, darting after Zabini as quietly as possible, though the rattling of the train made such caution almost pointless.

The corridors were almost completely empty now. Nearly everyone had returned to their carriages to change into their school robes and pack up their possessions.

Though he was as close as he could get to Zabini without touching him, Harry was not quick enough to slip into the compartment when Zabini opened the door. Zabini was already sliding it shut when Harry hastily stuck out his foot to prevent it closing.

“What’s wrong with this thing?” said Zabini angrily as he smashed the sliding door repeatedly into Harry’s foot.

Harry seized the door and pushed it open, hard; Zabini, still clinging on to the handle, toppled over sideways into **Gregory Goyle’s** lap, and in the ensuing ruckus, Harry darted into the compartment, leapt onto Zabini’s temporarily empty seat, and hoisted himself up into the luggage rack.

It was fortunate that Goyle and Zabini were snarling at each other, drawing all eyes onto them, for Harry was quite sure his feet and ankles had been revealed as the cloak had flapped around them; indeed, for one horrible moment he thought he saw **Malfoy’s** eyes follow his trainer as it whipped upward out of sight.

But then Goyle slammed the door shut and flung Zabini off him; Zabini collapsed into his own seat looking ruffled, **Vincent Crabbe** returned to his comic, and Malfoy, sniggering, lay back down across two seats with his head in **Pansy Parkinson’s** lap.

Harry lay curled uncomfortably under the cloak to ensure that every inch of him remained hidden, and watched Pansy stroke the sleek blond hair off Malfoy’s forehead, smirking as she did so, as though anyone would have loved to have been in her place.

The lanterns swinging from the carriage ceiling cast a bright light over the scene: Harry could read every word of Crabbe’s comic directly below him.

## Malfoy and Zabini’s Conversation

“So, Zabini,” said Malfoy, “what did Slughorn want?”

“Just trying to make up to well-connected people,” said Zabini, who was still glowering at Goyle. “Not that he managed to find many.”

This information did not seem to please Malfoy. “Who else had he invited?” he demanded.

“McLaggen from Gryffindor,” said Zabini.

“Oh yeah, his uncle’s big in the Ministry,” said Malfoy.

“—someone else called Belby, from Ravenclaw—”

“Not him, he’s a prat!” said Pansy.

“—and Longbottom, Potter, and that Weasley girl,” finished Zabini.

Malfoy sat up very suddenly, knocking Pansy’s hand aside.

“He invited Longbottom?”

“Well, I assume so, as Longbottom was there,” said Zabini indifferently.

“What’s Longbottom got to interest Slughorn?”

Zabini shrugged.

“Potter, precious Potter, obviously he wanted a look at the Chosen One,” sneered Malfoy, “but that Weasley girl! What’s so special about her?”

## Draco Malfoy's Conversation on the Train

**Pansy Parkinson** observed **Draco Malfoy** closely, commenting on his opinion about a girl many boys liked. **Blaise Zabini** responded coldly, showing disdain for her due to her being a **blood traitor**.

- Malfoy appeared relaxed as Pansy stroked his hair.
- Pansy criticized **Professor Slughorn's** taste, suggesting he might be senile.
- Malfoy mentioned his father's connection to Slughorn and hinted at not expecting an invitation for the next school year.

Zabini discussed Slughorn's lack of interest in **Death Eaters**, recalling an instance when Slughorn was unhappy about the arrest of Nott's father.

Malfoy reacted with anger but dismissed Slughorn as "just some stupid teacher," suggesting he might not return to **Hogwarts** next year.

## Malfoy's Future Plans

When questioned, Malfoy hinted that he might be moving on to "bigger and better things."

- He expressed skepticism about the importance of formal education.
- Suggested that when **the Dark Lord** takes over, qualifications like **O.W.L.s** or **N.E.W.T.s** won't matter.
- Emphasized that allegiance and devotion to the Dark Lord will be valued more.

Zabini doubted Malfoy's abilities due to his young age and incomplete education, but Malfoy countered that the job might not require formal qualifications.

Malfoy then pointed out the view of **Hogwarts** through the window and told others to get their robes on.

## Harry's Hidden Presence and Malfoy's Attack

Harry, hidden under his **Invisibility Cloak** in the luggage rack, was watching all this unfold.

- He was startled when Goyle accidentally hit him with a trunk.
- Dreaded being discovered by the group of **Slytherins**.
- Malfoy eventually closed the compartment blinds and revealed hidden intentions.

Suddenly, Malfoy cast **"Petrificus Totalus"**, paralyzing Harry and causing him to fall out of the luggage rack.

- Harry was immobilized and exposed, his cloak trapped beneath him.
- Malfoy confronted Harry, revealing he'd seen several suspicious movements.
- He accused Harry of blocking the door and confirmed his suspicions about Harry's presence.

Malfoy then stomped on Harry's face, breaking his nose and causing bleeding.

- Malfoy placed the cloak back over Harry, coldly stating no one would find him until the train reached London.
- He deliberately stepped on Harry's fingers before leaving the compartment.

## 8. SNAPE VICTORIOUS

Harry lay helpless under the cloak, feeling the blood from his broken nose.

- He realized no one seemed to notice he was missing.
- Tried unsuccessfully to summon his wand with **"Accio Wand!"** silently.
- Felt hopeless as the train moved away from the station.

Suddenly, his cloak was pulled off, and a voice greeted him.

- A **flash of red light** freed Harry from paralysis.
- **Nymphadora Tonks** appeared, helped Harry to sit up, and returned his cloak.
- Tonks suggested they leave the train immediately by jumping off.

Harry followed Tonks as the train accelerated away.

- The cold night air soothed his throbbing nose.
- Tonks offered to heal his injury using magic.

She cast the healing spell **"Episkey"**, fixing Harry's broken nose.

- Harry thanked her gratefully.
- Tonks urged him to put the cloak back on.

## Tonks’ Patronus and Explanation

Tonks summoned a large silver animal with her wand.

- Harry recognized it as a **Patronus**.
- Tonks explained she sent a message to Hogwarts to alert them that she had Harry, preventing worry.

They began walking toward the lane leading to the school.

Harry asked how Tonks found him.

- She explained she noticed his absence from the train and suspected he was hiding.
- The drawn blinds signaled to her to check the compartment.

Tonks revealed she was stationed in **Hogsmeade** to provide extra protection for the school.

- Other **Aurors** stationed there included **Proudfoot**, **Savage**, and **Dawlish**.
- Harry recognized Dawlish as the Auror involved in an incident with **Dumbledore** the prior year.

## Hogwarts Arrival and Encounter with Snape

They trudged up the dark, deserted lane, following the freshly made carriage tracks. **Harry** looked sideways at **Tonks** under his cloak. Last year she had been inquisitive (to the point of being a little annoying at times), laughed easily, and made jokes. Now she seemed older and much more serious and purposeful. Was this all the effect of what had happened at the **Ministry**?

He reflected uncomfortably that **Hermione** would have suggested he say something consoling about **Sirius** to her, that it wasn’t her fault at all, but he couldn’t bring himself to do it. He was far from blaming her for Sirius’s death; it was no more her fault than anyone else’s (and much less than his), but he did not like talking about **Sirius** if he could avoid it.

And so they tramped on through the cold night in silence, Tonks’s long cloak whispering on the ground behind them.

Having always traveled there by carriage, **Harry** had never before appreciated just how far **Hogwarts** was from **Hogsmeade Station**. With great relief, he finally saw the tall pillars on either side of the gates, each topped with a **winged boar**. He was cold, hungry, and eager to leave this new, gloomy **Tonks** behind.

When he put out a hand to push open the gates, he found them chained shut.

“Alohomora!” he said confidently, pointing his wand at the padlock, but nothing happened.

“That won’t work on these,” said Tonks. “**Dumbledore** bewitched them himself.”

Harry looked around. “I could climb a wall,” he suggested.

“No, you couldn’t,” said Tonks flatly. “Anti-intruder jinxes on all of them. Security’s been tightened a hundredfold this summer.”

“Well then,” said Harry, starting to feel annoyed at her lack of helpfulness, “I suppose I’ll just have to sleep out here and wait for morning.”

“Someone’s coming down for you,” said Tonks, “Look.”

A lantern was bobbing at the distant foot of the castle. Harry was so pleased to see it he felt he could even endure **Filch’s** wheezy criticisms and rants about his tardiness. It was not until the glowing yellow light was ten feet away and had pulled off his **Invisibility Cloak** so he could be seen, that he recognized, with a rush of pure loathing, the uplit hooked nose and long, black, greasy hair of **Severus Snape**.

“Well, well, well,” sneered Snape, taking out his wand and tapping the padlock once, so the chains snaked backward and the gates creaked open. “Nice of you to turn up, Potter, although you have evidently decided that the wearing of school robes would detract from your appearance.”

“I couldn’t change, I didn’t have my—” Harry began, but Snape cut across him.

“There is no need to wait, **Nymphadora**, Potter is quite—ah—safe in my hands.”

“I meant **Hagrid** to get the message,” said Tonks, frowning.

“Hagrid was late for the start-of-term feast, just like Potter here, so I took it instead. And incidentally,” said Snape, stepping aside, “I was interested to see your new **Patronus**.”

He shut the gates in her face with a loud clang and tapped the chains again, which slithered back into place.

“I think you were better off with the old one,” said Snape, his voice dripping with malice. “The new one looks weak.”

As Snape swung the lantern about, Harry saw a fleeting look of shock and anger on Tonks’s face before she was swallowed by darkness.

“Good night,” Harry called over his shoulder, beginning the walk up to the school with Snape. “Thanks for… everything.”

“See you, Harry.”

Snape did not speak for a minute or so. Harry felt his body generating waves of hatred so powerful it seemed incredible Snape could not feel them burning him. He had loathed Snape since their first encounter, but Snape had placed himself forever and irrevocably beyond forgiveness by his attitude toward **Sirius**.

Harry had concluded over the summer that Snape’s snide remarks to Sirius about staying safely hidden while the rest of the **Order of the Phoenix** were fighting **Voldemort** had likely contributed to Sirius rushing to the Ministry the night he died. Harry clung to this notion for the satisfaction of blame and because he knew Snape was not sorry for Sirius’s death.

“Fifty points from Gryffindor for lateness, I think,” said Snape. “And let me see, another twenty for your Muggle attire. You know, I don’t believe any House has ever been in negative figures this early in the term—we haven’t even started pudding. You might have set a record, Potter.”

The fury inside Harry blazed white-hot, but he would have preferred to be immobilized than tell Snape why he was late.

“I suppose you wanted to make an entrance, did you?” Snape continued. “And with no flying car available you decided that bursting into the Great Hall halfway through the feast ought to create a dramatic effect.”

Still Harry remained silent, his chest burning. He knew Snape had come to needle and torment him in these few minutes without an audience.

They reached the castle steps, and the great oaken front doors swung open into the vast flagged entrance hall, where a burst of talk and laughter and tinkling of plates welcomed them through the doors into the Great Hall.

Harry wondered if he could slip his **Invisibility Cloak** back on and gain his seat at the long **Gryffindor table** unnoticed.

“No cloak,” Snape said as though reading Harry’s mind. “You can walk in so that everyone sees you, which is what you wanted, I’m sure.”

Harry turned and marched through the open doors, anything to get away from Snape.

## The Great Hall and Friends

The **Great Hall** with its four long House tables and staff table at the top was decorated as usual with floating candles that made the plates glitter and glow. It was all a shimmering blur to Harry as he walked fast enough to pass the **Hufflepuff table** before people started staring.

By the time they stood up to get a good look at him, Harry spotted **Ron** and **Hermione**, sped along the benches toward them, and forced his way in between them.

“Where’ve you—blimey, what’ve you done to your face?” said Ron, staring at the blood covering Harry.

“Why, what’s wrong with it?” said Harry, grabbing a spoon and squinting at his distorted reflection.

“You’re covered in blood!” said Hermione, raising her wand and saying “**Tergeo!**” to siphon off the dried blood.

“Thanks,” said Harry, feeling his now clean face. “How’s my nose looking?”

“Normal,” said Hermione anxiously. “Why shouldn’t it? Harry, what happened? We’ve been terrified!”

“I’ll tell you later

## Scene: Harry and Hermione Discuss the Injury

**Harry** whispered to **Hermione**, “His hand was like that when I saw him over the summer. I thought he’d have cured it by now, though… or Madam Pomfrey would’ve done.”

“It looks as if it’s **died**,” said Hermione with a nauseated expression. “But there are some injuries you can’t cure… old curses… and there are poisons without antidotes…”

---

## Announcements in the Great Hall

- **Mr. Filch**, the caretaker, announced a **blanket ban on joke items** from **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**.
- Students wishing to play for **House Quidditch teams** should give their names to their **Heads of House** as usual.
- Hogwarts is also seeking new **Quidditch commentators**.

---

## New Staff Introductions

- **Professor Slughorn** was introduced as the new **Potions master**.  
  Described as a former colleague of Dumbledore, Slughorn stood up amid applause.

- There was surprise when it was announced that **Professor Snape** would take the position of **Defense Against the Dark Arts teacher**.

---

## Student Reactions to Staff Changes

- **Harry** reacted loudly in disbelief at Snape's appointment, having thought Slughorn would teach Defense Against the Dark Arts.
- **Ron** and **Hermione** both expressed surprise, questioning Harry’s information.

Snape, seated beside Dumbledore, acknowledged applause lazily, showing a triumphant look.

**Harry:** “Well, there’s one good thing. Snape’ll be gone by the end of the year.”

**Ron:** Explained the **job’s jinxed** nature, no one lasts more than a year; **Quirrell died doing it**. He hopes Snape might return to Potions.

---

## Dumbledore’s Warning and Closing of the Feast

- **Lord Voldemort and his followers** are once again free and growing stronger.
- Hogwarts castle’s magical fortifications have been **strengthened**.
- Students must follow **security restrictions**, especially regarding **after hours curfew**.
- Any suspicious behavior must be reported immediately.
- Dumbledore urged students to conduct themselves with care for their own and others’ safety.

Dumbledore ended the feast with **“Pip pip!”** before the students left the Hall.

---

## Harry, Ron, and Hermione Outside the Hall

- Harry delayed leaving to avoid **Malfoy**, overhearing Malfoy boasting about a mysterious **mission** potentially linked to Voldemort.
- Ron dismissed Malfoy’s bragging as showing off for **Parkinson**.
- Harry worried about Voldemort’s influence within Hogwarts.

---

## Interaction with Hagrid

- Hagrid appeared, having been **late** due to spending time with his giant half-brother, **Grawp**, who now lives in a **cave in the mountains**, arranged by Dumbledore.
- Hagrid is hopeful about training Grawp as his assistant.
- Hagrid reminded Harry and Ron about the first lesson the next day.

Ron expressed relief to avoid **Care of Magical Creatures**, a subject both he and Harry have really no intention of continuing, much to Hagrid’s probable disappointment.

---

## 9. THE HALF-BLOOD PRINCE

### Morning in the Common Room

- Harry and Ron shared their concerns about Malfoy’s overheard words with Hermione.
- Hermione was unsure whether Malfoy was lying or boasting.
- They attracted attention, with Ron telling off a rude first-year boy.
- Ron expressed excitement about **free time** this year to relax, but Hermione reminded them of study responsibilities.

---

### Incident with Fanged Frisbees

- Hermione stopped a student from bringing a **Fanged Frisbee**, which are banned.
- Ron opportunistically claimed he had always wanted one, amusing **Lavender Brown**.

---

### Breakfast and Class Schedules

- The Great Hall ceiling was calm and blue during breakfast.
- Harry and Ron confided in Hermione about their awkward conversation with Hagrid.
- Hermione doubted they would continue in **Care of Magical Creatures**.

---

### Professor McGonagall’s Role

- McGonagall distributed **class schedules** based on whether students had the necessary **O.W.L. grades** for their chosen **N.E.W.T. subjects**.
- Hermione was immediately cleared to continue multiple subjects including **Charms, Defense Against the Dark Arts, Transfiguration, Herbology, Arithmancy, Ancient Runes, and Potions**.
- Neville took longer to be sorted, looking anxious as McGonagall examined his results.

## Professor McGonagall's Assessment of Neville Longbottom

- Neville qualified for **O.W.L.** with an **‘Outstanding’** in **Herbology**.
- He achieved **‘Exceeds Expectations’** in **Defense Against the Dark Arts**.
- Neville received an **‘Acceptable’** in **Transfiguration**, which was insufficient to continue to **N.E.W.T.** level.
- Professor McGonagall expressed concern about Neville coping with the **Transfiguration** coursework.

### Discussion about Neville's Ambitions

- Neville’s grandmother wished him to continue **Transfiguration**.
- Professor McGonagall urged Neville to focus on his strengths and suggested **Charms** as an alternative **N.E.W.T.** subject.
- The professor promised to inform Neville’s grandmother that **Charms** is a valuable subject, despite her previous failure.

---

## Scheduling Classes

### Parvati Patil’s Divination Classes

- **Firenze** and **Professor Trelawney** are sharing **Divination** teaching duties.
- The sixth year classes in **Divination** are handled by Professor Trelawney.
- Parvati appeared slightly disappointed about this arrangement.

### Harry Potter’s Schedule and Subjects

- Harry passed in **Charms**, **Defense Against the Dark Arts**, **Herbology**, and **Transfiguration**.
- He was advised to continue with **Potions** despite not purchasing materials yet.
- **Professor Slughorn** accepts **N.E.W.T.** students with **‘Exceeds Expectations’** in **Potions**.
- Harry was informed about **Gryffindor Quidditch** team trials.

### Ron Weasley’s Schedule

- Ron’s subjects matched Harry’s.
- Both noted they had several free periods in their schedules.

---

## Gryffindor Common Room Interaction

- **Katie Bell**, the original Gryffindor Quidditch team member, congratulated Harry on his captaincy.
- Katie emphasized the importance of fair **team trials** to welcome potentially better players.
- Ron became quiet, playing with the **Fanged Frisbee**, which irritated **Crookshanks** the cat.

---

## Defense Against the Dark Arts Class with Professor Snape

### Class Atmosphere

- The classroom was gloomy, lit by candlelight with drawn curtains.
- **Gruesome pictures** depicting injuries and magical curses adorned the walls.
- Silence followed Professor Snape's entrance.

### Snape’s Speech and Perspective

- Snape acknowledged the turnover of five previous teachers in the subject.
- He emphasized the challenge of the **Dark Arts** as a **many-headed monster**, continuously evolving.
- Defenses must be **flexible** and **inventive** to combat such dangers.
- Pictures on the walls showed victims of the **Cruciatus Curse**, the **Dementor’s Kiss**, and **Inferius** attacks.

### Class Questions and Warnings

- **Parvati Patil** asked about the use of **Inferi**.
- Snape confirmed the **Dark Lord** has used **Inferi** before and advised caution.

### Non-Verbal Spells Exercise

- Students were instructed to practice **non-verbal spells** in pairs.
- The advantage of non-verbal spells: giving the adversary no warning, granting a split-second tactical advantage.
- **Hermione Granger** gave this explanation, quoted from **The Standard Book of Spells, Grade Six**.
- Snape noted not all wizards can perform such spells due to the required concentration and mind power.

### Snape’s Demonstration and Harry’s Response

- Ron and Harry struggled with the exercise; Ron resisted muttering the incantation.
- Snape called Ron's effort **pathetic** and demonstrated using his wand on Harry.
- Harry instinctively cast **Protego** verbally, knocking Snape off balance.
- Snape reprimanded Harry for verbalizing the spell during non-verbal practice.
- Harry accidentally showed cheek by correcting Snape on addressing him as “sir.”
- Snape assigned Harry **detention** for this behavior.

---

## After Class Discussion

- Ron praised Harry’s defense.
- Hermione questioned Harry's defiance.
- Harry explained his reaction was due to repeated jinxing attempts during past **Occlumency lessons**.
- Harry expressed dismay at Snape's teaching and apparent fascination with the **Dark Arts**.
- Hermione remarked that Snape's passion sounded similar to Harry's own intensity.

## Private Lessons and Quidditch Trials

“Yes, when you were telling us what it’s like to face **Voldemort**, you said it wasn’t just memorizing a bunch of spells, you said it was just you and your brains and your guts—well, wasn’t that what **Snape** was saying? That it really comes down to being **brave** and **quick-thinking**?”

Harry was so disarmed that he thought the words were as worth memorizing as *The Standard Book of Spells* and did not argue.

“Harry! Hey, Harry!”

Harry looked around; **Jack Sloper**, one of the Beaters on last year’s **Gryffindor Quidditch** team, was hurrying toward him holding a roll of parchment.

“For you,” panted Sloper. “Listen, I heard you’re the new **Captain**. When’re you holding trials?”

“I’m not sure yet,” said Harry, thinking privately that Sloper would be very lucky to get back on the team. “I’ll let you know.”

“Oh, right. I was hoping it’d be this weekend—”

But Harry was not listening; he had just recognized the thin, slanting writing on the parchment. Leaving Sloper in mid-sentence, he hurried away with Ron and Hermione, unrolling the parchment as he went.

---

## Letter from Dumbledore

Dear Harry,

I would like to start our **private lessons** this **Saturday**. Kindly come along to my office at **8 P.M.** I hope you are enjoying your first day back at school.

Yours sincerely,  
**Albus Dumbledore**

P.S. I enjoy **Acid Pops**.

---

### The Password and Speculations

“He enjoys **Acid Pops**?” said Ron, who had read the message over Harry’s shoulder and was looking perplexed.

“It’s the **password** to get past the gargoyle outside his study,” said Harry in a low voice. “Ha! Snape’s not going to be pleased… I won’t be able to do his detention!”

He, Ron, and Hermione spent the whole of break speculating on what **Dumbledore** would teach Harry.  

- Ron thought it most likely to be spectacular **jinxes** and **hexes** unknown to the Death Eaters.  
- Hermione said such things were **illegal** and thought it more likely that Dumbledore wanted to teach advanced **Defensive magic**.  

After break, Hermione went off to **Arithmancy** while Harry and Ron grudgingly started **Snape’s homework**. The homework was so complex that they still had not finished when Hermione joined them for their after-lunch free period (though she considerably sped up the process). They had only just finished when the bell rang for the afternoon’s double **Potions** class.

---

## N.E.W.T. Potions Class with Slughorn

When they arrived in the corridor, only a dozen students were progressing to **N.E.W.T.** level. **Crabbe** and **Goyle** had failed to achieve the required **O.W.L.** grade, but four **Slytherins** had made it through, including **Malfoy**. Four **Ravenclaws** and one **Hufflepuff**, **Ernie Macmillan**, were also present.

“**Harry**,” Ernie said portentously, “didn’t get a chance to speak in Defense Against The Dark Arts this morning. Good lesson, I thought. Shield Charms are old hat for us old D.A. lags… And how are you, Ron—Hermione?”

Before they could reply, the dungeon door opened and **Professor Slughorn** entered, his great walrus mustache curving above a beaming mouth. He greeted Harry and **Zabini** with particular enthusiasm.

---

### Classroom Atmosphere

The dungeon was full of **vapors** and **odd smells**. Harry, Ron, and Hermione sniffed as they passed large, bubbling cauldrons. The four Slytherins and four Ravenclaws sat together, leaving Harry, Ron, Hermione, and Ernie to share a table near a gold-colored cauldron emitting a seductive scent.

The potion’s fumes filled Harry with **contentment**, and he exchanged lazy grins with Ron.

---

### Slughorn’s Instructions

“Now then, now then, now then,” said Slughorn, “**Scales out**, everyone, potion kits, and don’t forget your copies of *Advanced Potion-Making*…”

“Sir?” Harry raised his hand.

“Harry, m’boy?”

“I haven’t got a book or scales or anything—nor has Ron—we didn’t realize we’d be able to do the N.E.W.T., you see—”

“Ah, yes, Professor McGonagall did mention… not to worry. Use ingredients from the **store cupboard** today. I’ll lend you scales and some old books until you can get new ones from **Flourish and Blotts**.”

Slughorn fetched two battered copies of *Advanced Potion-Making* by **Libatius Borage** and two sets of tarnished scales for Harry and Ron.

---

## Magical Potions Introduced

Slughorn presented a few potions to the class, potions they ought to know after N.E.W.T.s.

- Nearest the Slytherin table was a cauldron of **boiling water**.  
- Hermione quickly identified it as **Veritaserum**, a colorless, odorless potion that forces the drinker to tell the truth.

“Very good!”

- Next was a slow-bubbling, mudlike cauldron that Hermione identified as **Polyjuice Potion** — a potion allowing one to assume someone else’s form.

- Another cauldron was pointed out as **Amortentia**, the most powerful **love potion** in the world. Hermione described its mother-of-pearl sheen, its steam spirals, and distinctive smell different to each person.  

Slughorn asked Hermione her name. When she replied **Hermione Granger**, he inquired if she was related to **Hector Dagworth-Granger**, founder of the **Most Extraordinary Society of Potioneers**. Hermione replied she was **Muggle-born**, with no relation.

Harry noticed Malfoy and Nott whispering and sniggering, but Slughorn only beamed.

“Oh! One of my best friends is Muggle-born, and she’s the best in our year!” he said, assuming Harry had spoken of Hermione. Hermione received **twenty points** for Gryffindor.

---

### Discussion on Amortentia

Slughorn explained that **Amortentia** does not create real love but causes **infatuation** or **obsession**, making it the most dangerous and powerful potion in the room.

---

## Felix Felicis: Liquid Luck

Ernie Macmillan pointed at a small black cauldron on Slughorn’s desk containing a golden potion splashing like goldfish.

“Ah,” said Slughorn, “this is **Felix Felicis**.”

Hermione gasped.

“It’s **liquid luck**, sir! It makes you lucky!”

Points were awarded, and the class paid attention.

Slughorn described Felix Felicis as:

- **Desperately tricky to make** and dangerous if made incorrectly  
- When brewed correctly, it causes all endeavors to **succeed** until the effects wear off  
- Not for constant use because excess causes **giddiness**, **recklessness**, and **dangerous overconfidence**  
- **Highly toxic** in large quantities  
- Best used **sparingly and occasionally**

When asked if he had ever taken it, Slughorn said he took it twice in his life, each time producing "two perfect days."

---

### Prize Announcement and Warnings

Slughorn revealed a tiny bottle of Felix Felicis as the prize for the lesson, enough for **twelve hours’ luck**.

- The winner could be lucky in everything they attempted from **dawn till dusk**.  
- Felix Felicis is a **banned substance** in organized competitions such as **sports**, **examinations**, or **elections**.  
- The winner must use it on an **ordinary day** only and watch how the ordinary becomes **extraordinary**.

## The Draught of Living Death Competition

“So,” said **Slughorn**, suddenly brisk, “how are you to win this fabulous prize? Well, by turning to page ten of **Advanced Potion-making**. We have a little over an hour left to us, which should be time for you to make a decent attempt at the **Draught of Living Death**. I know it is more complex than anything you have attempted before, and I do not expect a perfect potion from anybody. The person who does best, however, will win little **Felix** here. Off you go!”

There was a scraping as everyone drew their cauldrons toward them and some loud clunks as people began adding weights to their scales, but nobody spoke. The concentration within the room was almost tangible. Harry saw **Malfoy** riffling feverishly through his copy of **Advanced Potion-Making**. It could not have been clearer that Malfoy really wanted that lucky day. Harry bent swiftly over the tattered book Slughorn had lent him.

To his annoyance, he saw that the previous owner had scribbled all over the pages, so that the margins were as black as the printed portions. Bending low to decipher the ingredients (even here, the previous owner had made annotations and crossed things out) Harry hurried off toward the store cupboard to find what he needed. As he dashed back to his cauldron, he saw Malfoy cutting up **Valerian roots** as fast as he could.

Everyone kept glancing around at what the rest of the class was doing; this was both an advantage and a disadvantage of **Potions**, that it was hard to keep your work private. Within ten minutes, the whole place was full of bluish steam. **Hermione**, of course, seemed to have progressed furthest. Her potion already resembled the “smooth, blackcurrant-colored liquid” mentioned as the ideal halfway stage.

Having finished chopping his roots, Harry bent low over his book again. It was really very irritating, having to try and decipher the directions under all the stupid scribbles of the previous owner, who for some reason had taken issue with the order to cut up the **sopophorous bean** and had written in the alternative instruction:

**Crush with flat side of silver dagger, releases juice better than cutting.**

---

## Interaction Between Malfoy and Slughorn

“Sir, I think you knew my grandfather, **Abraxas Malfoy**?”

Harry looked up; Slughorn was just passing the **Slytherin** table.

“Yes,” said Slughorn, without looking at Malfoy, “I was sorry to hear he had died, although of course it wasn’t unexpected, **dragon pox** at his age…”

And he walked away. Harry bent back over his cauldron, smirking. He could tell that Malfoy had expected to be treated like Harry or Zabini; perhaps even hoped for some preferential treatment of the type he had learned to expect from Snape. It looked as though Malfoy would have to rely on nothing but **talent** to win the bottle of **Felix Felicis**.

The sopophorous bean was proving very difficult to cut up. Harry turned to Hermione.

“Can I borrow your silver knife?”

She nodded impatiently, not taking her eyes off her potion, which was still deep purple, though according to the book ought to be turning a light shade of lilac by now.

Harry crushed his bean with the flat side of the dagger. To his astonishment, it immediately exuded so much **juice** he was amazed the shriveled bean could have held it all.

Hastily scooping it all into the cauldron he saw, to his surprise, that the potion immediately turned exactly the shade of **lilac** described by the textbook.

His annoyance with the previous owner vanishing on the spot, Harry now squinted at the next line of instructions. According to the book, he had to stir **counterclockwise** until the potion turned clear as water. According to the addition the previous owner made, however, he ought to add a **clockwise stir after every seventh counterclockwise stir**. Could the old owner be right twice?

Harry stirred counterclockwise, held his breath, and stirred once clockwise. The effect was immediate. The potion turned **pale pink**.

---

## Hermione’s Reaction and Further Instructions

“How are you doing that?” demanded **Hermione**, who was red-faced and whose hair was growing bushier and bushier in the fumes from her cauldron; her potion was still resolutely purple.

“Add a clockwise stir—”

“No, no, the book says counterclockwise!” she snapped.

Harry shrugged and continued what he was doing:  

- Seven stirs counterclockwise  
- One clockwise  
- Pause  
- Repeat

Across the table, **Ron** was cursing fluently under his breath; his potion looked like liquid licorice. Harry glanced around. As far as he could see, no one else’s potion had turned as pale as his. He felt elated, something that had certainly never happened before in this dungeon.

---

## Conclusion of the Potion Competition

“And time’s… up!” called Slughorn. “Stop stirring, please!”

Slughorn moved slowly among the tables, peering into cauldrons. He made no comment, but occasionally gave the potions a stir or a sniff. At last he reached the table where Harry, Ron, Hermione, and Ernie were sitting. He smiled ruefully at the tarlike substance in Ron’s cauldron. He passed over Ernie’s navy concoction. Hermione’s potion he gave an approving nod. Then he saw Harry’s, and a look of **incredulous delight** spread over his face.

“The clear winner!” he cried to the dungeon. “Excellent, excellent, Harry! Good lord, it’s clear you’ve inherited your mother’s talent. She was a dab hand at Potions, **Lily** was! Here you are, then, here you are—one bottle of **Felix Felicis**, as promised, and use it well!”

Harry slipped the tiny bottle of golden liquid into his inner pocket, feeling an odd combination of delight at the furious looks on the **Slytherins’** faces and guilt at the disappointed expression on Hermione’s. Ron looked simply dumbfounded.

---

## After the Competition: Reactions and Discoveries

“How did you do that?” he whispered to Harry as they left the dungeon.

“Got lucky, I suppose,” said Harry, because Malfoy was within earshot.

Once they were securely ensconced at the Gryffindor table for dinner, however, he felt safe enough to tell them. Hermione’s face became stonier with every word he uttered.

“I s’pose you think I cheated?” he finished, aggravated by her expression.

“Well, it wasn’t exactly your own work, was it?” she said stiffly.

“He only followed different instructions to ours,” said Ron, “Could’ve been a catastrophe, couldn’t it? But he took a risk and it paid off.” He heaved a sigh. “Slughorn could’ve handed me that book, but no, I get the one no one’s ever written on. Puked on, by the look of page fifty-two, but—”

“Hang on,” said a voice close by Harry’s left ear and he caught a sudden waft of that flowery smell he had picked up in Slughorn’s dungeon. He looked around and saw that **Ginny** had joined them. “Did I hear right? You’ve been taking orders from something someone wrote in a book, Harry?”

She looked alarmed and angry. Harry knew what was on her mind at once.

“It’s nothing,” he said reassuringly, lowering his voice. “It’s not like, you know, **Riddle’s diary**. It’s just an old textbook someone’s scribbled on.”

“But you’re doing what it says?”

“I just tried a few of the tips written in the margins, honestly, Ginny, there’s nothing funny—”

“Ginny’s got a point,” said Hermione, perking up at once. “We ought to check that there’s nothing odd about it. I mean, all these funny instructions, who knows?”

“Hey!” said Harry indignantly, as she pulled his copy of **Advanced Potion-Making** out of his bag and raised her wand.

---

## Inspecting the Textbook

“**Specialis Revelio!**” she said, rapping it smartly on the front cover. Nothing whatsoever happened. The book simply lay there, looking old and dirty and dog-eared.

“Finished?” said Harry irritably. “Or d’you want to wait and see if it does a few backflips?”

“It seems all right,” said Hermione, still staring at the book suspiciously. “I mean, it really does seem to be… just a textbook.”

“Good. Then I’ll have it back,” said Harry, snatching it off the table, but it slipped from his hand and landed open on the floor. Nobody else was looking. Harry bent low to retrieve the book, and as he did so, he saw something scribbled along the bottom of the back cover in the same small, cramped handwriting as the instructions that had won him his bottle of **Felix Felicis**, now safely hidden inside a pair of socks in his trunk upstairs.

**This book is the property of the Half Blood Prince.**

---

## 10. THE HOUSE OF GAUNT

For the rest of the week’s **Potions lessons** Harry continued to follow the **Half-Blood Prince’s** instructions wherever they deviated from **Libatius Borage’s**, with the result that by their fourth lesson **Slughorn** was raving about Harry’s abilities, saying that he had rarely taught anyone so talented. Neither Ron nor Hermione was delighted by this.

Although Harry had offered to share his book with both of them, Ron had more difficulty deciphering the handwriting than Harry did, and could not keep asking Harry to read aloud or it might look suspicious. Hermione, meanwhile, was resolutely plowing on with what she called the “official” instructions, but becoming increasingly bad-tempered as they yielded poorer results than the Prince’s.

Harry wondered vaguely who the **Half-Blood Prince** had been. Although the amount of homework they had been given prevented him from reading the whole of his copy of **Advanced Potion-Making**, he had skimmed through it sufficiently to see that there was barely a page on which the Prince had not made additional notes, not all of them concerned with potion-making. Here and there were directions for what looked like spells that the Prince had made up himself.

“Or herself,” said Hermione irritably, overhearing Harry pointing some of these out to Ron in the common room on Saturday evening. “It might have been a girl. I think the handwriting looks more like a girl’s than a boy’s.”

“The Half-Blood Prince, he was called,” Harry said. “How many girls have been Princes?”

Hermione seemed to have no answer to this. She merely scowled and twitched her essay on **The Principles of Rematerialization** away from Ron, who was trying to read it upside down.
